i) in the direction the yacht is moving

cos40 x 350
= 268.12

ii) perpendicular to the direction in which the yacht is moving

cos50 x 350
= 224.98

b) For the boat to be at equilibrium, the sailor has to balance the force of the wind by causing an opposite moment on the other side of the boat in order to balance it. ^LvZvJdVg
